When a player plays an eight, he or she must declare the suit that the next player is to play. \r\nAs an example: Once the six of clubs is played the next player can: \r\n- play any of the other sixes \r\n- play any of the clubs \r\n- play any eight (must declare the suit) \r\n- draw from the stockpile \r\n\r\nPoints are incurred for any cards left on hand at the end of a round - 25pts for an eight, 10pts for a face card, and face value for a spot card.
